	trait = diligent
	trait = pensive

	disallow_random_traits = yes

	8219.1.1 = { 
		birth = yes 
		add_character_flag = canon_status_canon
	}
	8239.1.1 = { 
		trait = knight 
		trait = education_martial_prowess_2
	}
	8248.1.1 = { add_spouse = Royce_81 } # Jeyne Royce
	8255.1.1 = { add_spouse = Arryn_6 } # Rowena Arryn
	8278.10.1 = {
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { character:Baratheon_2 = { is_alive = yes } }
				set_relation_friend = { 
					target = character:Baratheon_2 # Robert Baratheon
					reason = friend_child_care
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { character:Stark_3 = { is_alive = yes } }
				set_relation_friend = { 
					target = character:Stark_3 # Eddard Stark
					reason = friend_child_care
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8282.5.1 = {
		add_spouse = Tully_6 # Lysa Tully
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { game_start_date = 8282.9.15 }
				add_character_flag = bookmark_independent
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					character:Tully_1 = { is_alive = yes } 
					character:Tully_6 = { is_alive = yes } 
				}
				create_alliance = { # By marriage
					target = character:Tully_1 # Hoster Tully
					allied_through_owner = ROOT # Jon Arryn
					allied_through_target = character:Tully_6 # Lysa Tully
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { character:Baratheon_2 = { is_alive = yes } }
				create_alliance = { # By friendship
					target = character:Baratheon_2 # Robert Baratheon
					allied_through_owner = ROOT # Jon Arryn
					allied_through_target = character:Baratheon_2 # Robert Baratheon
				}
				character:Baratheon_2 = {
					add_opinion = {
						target = ROOT
						modifier = perk_negotiated_alliance_opinion
					}
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { character:Stark_3 = { is_alive = yes } }
				create_alliance = { # By friendship
					target = character:Stark_3 # Eddard Stark
					allied_through_owner = ROOT # Jon Arryn
					allied_through_target = character:Stark_3 # Eddard Stark
				}
				character:Stark_3 = {
					add_opinion = {
						target = ROOT
						modifier = perk_negotiated_alliance_opinion
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8284.2.6 = { # Crowned Stag
		effect = {
			agot_appoint_as_councillor_for_castle_history_effect = { 
				CASTLE = title:e_the_iron_throne 
				POSITION = councillor_castellan
			}
			remove_variable = pre_war_liege
		}
	}
	8298.2.24 = {
		death = {
			death_reason = death_poison
			killer = Tully_6 # Lysa Tully
		}
	}
}
